  <raw>MARINERS DESIGNATE OLERUD FOR ASSIGNMENT



First baseman John Olerud, a two-time All-Star and three-time Gold Glove winner, was designated for assignment by the Seattle Mariners on Thursday. Olerud, 35, is hitting .245 with five homers and 22 RBIs.
Seattle has 10 days to release, trade or send Olerud to the minors. If he is released, the Mariners would be responsible for the remainder of his $7.7 million salary.

Last week, shortstop Rich Aurilia, 32, was designated for assignment.
Manager Bob Melvin said it was important for the Mariners, who are last in the A.L. West, to start playing younger players with a look toward 2005. Scott Spiezio will switch from third base to first, handing Justin Leone, 27, the third-base job.
Catcher Pat Borders also was designated for assignment and the Mariners promoted infielder Bucky Jacobsen from Triple-A Tacoma and activated catcher Miguel Olivo.
* Arizona placed right-hander Andrew Good and catcher Robby Hammock on the disabled list, promoted reliever Mike Fetters from Triple-A Tucson and activated catcher Brent Mayne.
* Detroit Tigers activated utilityman Brandon Inge, recalled left-hander Wilfredo Ledezma from Double-A Erie and placed outfielder Alex Sanchez on the D.L.
* Montreal activated right-hander John Patterson, recalled infielder Henry Mateo from Triple-A Edmonton and sent right-hander Shawn Hill to Double-A Harrisburg.
* Minnesota activated outfielder Shannon Stewart and placed first baseman Doug Mientkiewicz on the D.L. because of a sore wrist.
* Minnesota catcher Joe Mauer underwent an MRI exam on his left knee. Manager Ron Gardenhire said the test showed some inflammation and "a couple of hot spots." Mauer, who had surgery on the knee in April, is day to day.
* Boston activated right-hander Ramiro Mendoza and sent third baseman Kevin Youkilis to Triple-A Pawtucket.
* Cincinnati activated first baseman Sean Casey and optioned catcher Corky Miller to Triple-A Louisville.
* The New York Yankees placed right-hander Sam Marsonek on the D.L. because of a sore knee and recalled right-hander Juan Padilla from Triple-A Columbus.</raw>
